    57â†’/**
    58â†’ * Hook for Apple liquid glass magnetic hover effect

    60â†’export function useAppleLiquidGlass(options: AppleLiquidGlassOptions = {}) {
    61â†’  const elementRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);
    62â†’  const {
    63â†’    intensity = 'medium',
    64â†’    magneticStrength = 0.3,
    65â†’    liquidFlow = true,
    66â†’    enableHaptics = false,
    67â†’  } = options;
    68â†’
    69â†’  const handleMouseMove = useCallback((e: MouseEvent) => {
    70â†’    if (!elementRef.current) return;
    71â†’
    72â†’    const rect = elementRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    73â†’    const centerX = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
    74â†’    const centerY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
    75â†’    
    76â†’    const deltaX = (e.clientX - centerX) * magneticStrength;
    77â†’    const deltaY = (e.clientY - centerY) * magneticStrength;
    78â†’
    79â†’    elementRef.current.style.transform = `translate(${deltaX}px, ${deltaY}px) translateZ(0)`;
    80â†’    
    81â†’    if (liquidFlow) {
    82â†’      const afterElement = elementRef.current.querySelector('::after') as HTMLElement;
    83â†’      if (afterElement) {
    84â†’        afterElement.style.transform = `translate(${-deltaX * 0.5}px, ${-deltaY * 0.5}px)`;
    85â†’      }
    86â†’    }
    87â†’  }, [magneticStrength, liquidFlow]);
    88â†’
    89â†’  const handleMouseLeave = useCallback(() => {
    90â†’    if (!elementRef.current) return;
    91â†’    
    92â†’    elementRef.current.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px) translateZ(0)';
    93â†’    elementRef.current.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
    94â†’    
    95â†’    setTimeout(() => {
    96â†’      if (elementRef.current) {
    97â†’        elementRef.current.style.transition = '';
    98â†’      }
    99â†’    }, 500);
   100â†’
   101â†’    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   102â†’      navigator.vibrate(10);
   103â†’    }
   104â†’  }, [enableHaptics]);
   105â†’
   106â†’  const handleMouseEnter = useCallback(() => {
   107â†’    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   108â†’      navigator.vibrate(5);
   109â†’    }
   110â†’  }, [enableHaptics]);
   111â†’
   112â†’  useEffect(() => {
   113â†’    const element = elementRef.current;
   114â†’    if (!element) return;
   115â†’
   116â†’    element.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   117â†’    element.addEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   118â†’    element.addEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   119â†’
   120â†’    return () => {
   121â†’      element.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   122â†’      element.removeEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   123â†’      element.removeEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   124â†’    };
   125â†’  }, [handleMouseMove, handleMouseLeave, handleMouseEnter]);
   126â†’
   127â†’  return {
   128â†’    ref: elementRef,
   129â†’    variant: APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS[intensity],
   130â†’    shadow: APPLE_LIQUID_SHADOWS[intensity],
   131â†’    afterEffect: APPLE_LIQUID_AFTER_EFFECTS[intensity],
   132â†’  };
   133â†’}
   134â†’
   135â†’/**
   136â†’ * Generate Apple liquid glass CSS classes - Tailwind v4 Compatible
   137â†’ */
   138â†’export function getAppleLiquidGlassClass(
   139â†’  intensity: keyof typeof APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS = 'medium',
   140â†’  interactive = true
   141â†’): string {
   142â†’  const baseClass = 'apple-liquid-glass';
   143â†’  const intensityClass = intensity !== 'medium' ? `apple-liquid-glass--${intensity}` : '';
   144â†’  const interactiveClass = interactive ? 'apple-liquid-glass--interactive' : '';
   145â†’  
   146â†’  return [baseClass, intensityClass, interactiveClass].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
   147â†’}
   148â†’
   149â†’/**
   150â†’ * Apple liquid glass animation presets
   151â†’ */
   152â†’export const APPLE_LIQUID_ANIMATIONS = {
   153â†’  hover: {
   154â†’    transform: 'translateY(-2px)',
   155â†’    transition: 'all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   156â†’  },
   157â†’  active: {
   158â†’    transform: 'translateY(0px) scale(0.98)',
   159â†’    transition: 'all 0.15s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   160â†’  },
   161â†’  focus: {
   162â†’    boxShadow: '0 0 0 3px rgba(0, 122, 255, 0.3)',
   163â†’    transition: 'box-shadow 0.2s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   164â†’  },
   165â†’} as const;
```

   282â†’// Utility functions for token access
   283â†’export const getToken = (path: string) => {
   284â†’  const keys = path.split('.');
   285â†’  let current: any = liquidGlassTokens;
   286â†’
   287â†’  for (const key of keys) {
   288â†’    if (current && typeof current === 'object' && key in current) {
   289â†’      current = current[key];
   290â†’    } else {
   291â†’      return undefined;
   292â†’    }
   293â†’  }
   294â†’
   295â†’  return current;
   296â†’};
   297â†’
   298â†’export const getThemeToken = (theme: 'light' | 'dark', path: string) => {
   299â†’  const keys = path.split('.');
   300â†’  let current: any = glassThemes[theme];
   301â†’
   302â†’  for (const key of keys) {
   303â†’    if (current && typeof current === 'object' && key in current) {
   304â†’      current = current[key];
   305â†’    } else {
   306â†’      return undefined;
   307â†’    }
   308â†’  }
   309â†’
   310â†’  return current;
   311â†’};
   312â†’
   313â†’// CSS Custom Properties Generator
   314â†’export const generateCSSCustomProperties = (
   315â†’  theme: 'light' | 'dark' = 'light'
   316â†’) => {
   317â†’  const themeTokens = glassThemes[theme];
   318â†’  const cssVars: Record<string, string> = {};
   319â†’
   320â†’  // Generate CSS custom properties from theme tokens
   321â†’  Object.entries(themeTokens).forEach(([category, values]) => {
   322â†’    Object.entries(values).forEach(([key, value]) => {
   323â†’      cssVars[`--glass-${category}-${key}`] = value as string;
   324â†’    });
   325â†’  });
   326â†’
   327â†’  // Add spacing tokens
   328â†’  Object.entries(liquidGlassTokens.spacing).forEach(([key, value]) => {
   329â†’    cssVars[`--glass-spacing-${key}`] = value;
   330â†’  });
   331â†’
   332â†’  // Add blur tokens
   333â†’  Object.entries(liquidGlassTokens.blur).forEach(([key, value]) => {
   334â†’    cssVars[`--glass-blur-${key}`] = `blur(${value})`;
   335â†’  });
   336â†’
   337â†’  return cssVars;
   338â†’};
   339â†’
   340â†’// Export types for TypeScript support
   341â†’export type LiquidGlassTokens = typeof liquidGlassTokens;
   342â†’export type GlassThemes = typeof glassThemes;
   343â†’export type ComponentTokens = typeof componentTokens;
   344â†’export type ThemeMode = keyof typeof glassThemes;
   345â†’

Result:

```
1â†’import {
     2â†’  createContext,
     3â†’  useContext,
     4â†’  useEffect,
     5â†’  useRef,
     6â†’  useState,
     7â†’  useCallback,
     8â†’  useMemo,
     9â†’} from 'react';
    10â†’import { liquidGlassTokens } from '../lib/liquid-glass-tokens';
    11â†’
    12â†’export interface LiquidGlassConfig {
    13â†’  color?: string; // rgb string e.g. "255,255,255"
    14â†’  blur?: number; // px
    15â†’  saturation?: number; // percentage
    16â†’  opacity?: number; // 0-1
    17â†’  adaptToContent?: boolean; // Enable content-aware adaptation
    18â†’  specularHighlights?: boolean; // Enable specular highlights
    19â†’  magneticHover?: boolean; // Enable magnetic hover effects
    20â†’}
    21â†’
    22â†’export interface ContentAnalysis {
    23â†’  averageColor: string;
    24â†’  brightness: number;
    25â†’  contrast: number;
    26â†’  dominantHue: number;
    27â†’}
    28â†’
    29â†’const defaultConfig: Required<LiquidGlassConfig> = {
    30â†’  color: '255,255,255',
    31â†’  blur: 24,
    32â†’  saturation: 180,
    33â†’  opacity: 0.75,
    34â†’  adaptToContent: true,
    35â†’  specularHighlights: true,
    36â†’  magneticHover: false,
    37â†’};
    38â†’
    39â†’const LiquidGlassContext = createContext<
    40â†’  LiquidGlassConfig & {
    41â†’    contentAnalysis?: ContentAnalysis;
    42â†’    updateGlassStyle: (_analysis: ContentAnalysis) => void;
    43â†’  }
    44â†’>(defaultConfig as any);
    45â†’
    46â†’export function LiquidGlassProvider({
    47â†’  children,
    48â†’  config,
    49â†’}: {
    50â†’  children: React.ReactNode;
    51â†’  config?: LiquidGlassConfig;
    52â†’}) {
    53â†’  const merged = useMemo(() => ({ ...defaultConfig, ...config }), [config]);
    54â†’  const [contentAnalysis, setContentAnalysis] = useState<ContentAnalysis>();
    55â†’
    56â†’  const updateGlassStyle = useCallback(
    57â†’    (analysis: ContentAnalysis) => {
    58â†’      setContentAnalysis(analysis);
    59â†’
    60â†’      if (!merged.adaptToContent) return;
    61â†’
    62â†’      const root = document.documentElement;
    63â†’
    64â†’      // Adapt glass properties based on content analysis
    65â†’      const adaptedOpacity =
    66â†’        merged.opacity * (1 + (analysis.contrast - 0.5) * 0.3);
    67â†’      const adaptedBlur = merged.blur * (1 + (1 - analysis.brightness) * 0.2);
    68â†’      const adaptedSaturation =
    69â†’        merged.saturation * (1 + analysis.brightness * 0.1);
    70â†’
    71â†’      // Set adaptive properties
    72â†’      root.style.setProperty(
    73â†’        '--glass-opacity-adaptive',
    74â†’        String(Math.max(0.1, Math.min(0.9, adaptedOpacity)))
    75â†’      );
    76â†’      root.style.setProperty(
    77â†’        '--glass-blur-adaptive',
    78â†’        `${Math.max(8, Math.min(48, adaptedBlur))}px`
    79â†’      );
    80â†’      root.style.setProperty(
    81â†’        '--glass-saturation-adaptive',
    82â†’        `${Math.max(120, Math.min(250, adaptedSaturation))}%`
    83â†’      );
    84â†’
    85â†’      // Adapt color based on dominant hue
    86â†’      const hue = analysis.dominantHue;
    87â†’      const adaptedColor = `hsl(${hue}, 20%, ${analysis.brightness > 0.5 ? 95 : 15}%)`;
    88â†’      root.style.setProperty('--glass-color-adaptive', adaptedColor);
    89â†’    },
    90â†’    [merged]
    91â†’  );
    92â†’
    93â†’  useEffect(() => {
    94â†’    const root = document.documentElement;
    95â†’
    96â†’    // Set base properties
    97â†’    root.style.setProperty('--glass-color', `rgb(${merged.color})`);
    98â†’    root.style.setProperty('--glass-blur', `${merged.blur}px`);
    99â†’    root.style.setProperty('--glass-saturation', `${merged.saturation}%`);
   100â†’    root.style.setProperty('--glass-opacity', String(merged.opacity));
   101â†’
   102â†’    // Set liquid glass tokens
   103â†’    Object.entries(liquidGlassTokens.colors.glass.white).forEach(
   104â†’      ([key, value]) => {
   105â†’        root.style.setProperty(`--liquid-glass-${key}`, value as string);
   106â†’      }
   107â†’    );
   108â†’
   109â†’    // Set shadow tokens
   110â†’    Object.entries(liquidGlassTokens.shadows.glass).forEach(([key, value]) => {
   111â†’      root.style.setProperty(`--liquid-shadow-${key}`, value as string);
   112â†’    });
   113â†’
   114â†’    // Set timing tokens
   115â†’    Object.entries(liquidGlassTokens.animation.duration).forEach(
   116â†’      ([key, value]) => {
   117â†’        root.style.setProperty(`--liquid-timing-${key}`, value as string);
   118â†’      }
   119â†’    );
   120â†’
   121â†’    // Enable specular highlights if configured
   122â†’    if (merged.specularHighlights) {
   123â†’      root.style.setProperty('--specular-enabled', '1');
   124â†’    }
   125â†’  }, [merged]);
   126â†’
   127â†’  return (
   128â†’    <LiquidGlassContext.Provider
   129â†’      value={{ ...merged, contentAnalysis, updateGlassStyle }}
   130â†’    >
   131â†’      {children}
   132â†’    </LiquidGlassContext.Provider>
   133â†’  );
   134â†’}
   135â†’
   136â†’export const useLiquidGlass = () => useContext(LiquidGlassContext);
   137â†’
   138â†’// Content-aware glass hook
   139â†’export const useContentAwareGlass = (
   140â†’  contentRef: React.RefObject<HTMLElement>
   141â†’) => {
   142â†’  const { updateGlassStyle, adaptToContent } = useLiquidGlass();
   143â†’  const analysisRef = useRef<ContentAnalysis | null>(null);
   144â†’
   145â†’  const analyzeContent = useCallback(async () => {
   146â†’    if (!contentRef.current || !adaptToContent) return;
   147â†’
   148â†’    try {
   149â†’      const element = contentRef.current;
   150â†’      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
   151â†’      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
   152â†’
   153â†’      if (!ctx) return;
   154â†’
   155â†’      // Create a temporary canvas to analyze the content
   156â†’      const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();
   157â†’      canvas.width = Math.min(rect.width, 200);
   158â†’      canvas.height = Math.min(rect.height, 200);
   159â†’
   160â†’      // Capture element as image data (simplified approach)
   161â†’      const computedStyle = getComputedStyle(element);
   162â†’      const bgColor = computedStyle.backgroundColor;
   163â†’
   164â†’      // Parse background color and analyze
   165â†’      const analysis = analyzeColor(bgColor);
   166â†’
   167â†’      if (
   168â†’        analysis &&
   169â†’        JSON.stringify(analysis) !== JSON.stringify(analysisRef.current)
   170â†’      ) {
   171â†’        analysisRef.current = analysis;
   172â†’        updateGlassStyle(analysis);
   173â†’      }
   174â†’    } catch (error) {
   175â†’      console.warn('Content analysis failed:', error);
   176â†’    }
   177â†’  }, [contentRef, updateGlassStyle, adaptToContent]);
   178â†’
   179â†’  useEffect(() => {
   180â†’    if (!adaptToContent) return;
   181â†’
   182â†’    const observer = new MutationObserver(analyzeContent);
   183â†’    const resizeObserver = new ResizeObserver(analyzeContent);
   184â†’
   185â†’    if (contentRef.current) {
   186â†’      observer.observe(contentRef.current, {
   187â†’        attributes: true,
   188â†’        childList: true,
   189â†’        subtree: true,
   190â†’        attributeFilter: ['style', 'class'],
   191â†’      });
   192â†’      resizeObserver.observe(contentRef.current);
   193â†’    }
   194â†’
   195â†’    // Initial analysis
   196â†’    analyzeContent();
   197â†’
   198â†’    return () => {
   199â†’      observer.disconnect();
   200â†’      resizeObserver.disconnect();
   201â†’    };
   202â†’  }, [analyzeContent, adaptToContent, contentRef]);
   203â†’
   204â†’  return analysisRef.current;
   205â†’};
   206â†’
   207â†’// Helper function to analyze color
   208â†’function analyzeColor(colorString: string): ContentAnalysis | null {
   209â†’  if (!colorString || typeof colorString !== 'string') {
   210â†’    console.warn('analyzeColor: Invalid color string provided:', colorString);
   211â†’    return null;
   212â†’  }
   213â†’
   214â†’  try {
   215â†’    // Parse RGB values from color string with better error handling
   216â†’    const rgbMatch = colorString.match(
   217â†’      /rgba?\((\d+),\s*(\d+),\s*(\d+)(?:,\s*([\d.]+))?\)/
   218â†’    );
   219â†’
   220â†’    if (!rgbMatch) {
   221â†’      console.warn('analyzeColor: Could not parse color string:', colorString);
   222â†’      // Return a default analysis for unrecognized colors
   223â†’      return {
   224â†’        averageColor: 'rgb(128, 128, 128)',
   225â†’        brightness: 0.5,
   226â†’        contrast: 0.5,
   227â†’        dominantHue: 0,
   228â†’      };
   229â†’    }
   230â†’
   231â†’    const r = parseInt(rgbMatch[1], 10) / 255;
   232â†’    const g = parseInt(rgbMatch[2], 10) / 255;
   233â†’    const b = parseInt(rgbMatch[3], 10) / 255;
   234â†’
   235â†’    // Validate parsed values
   236â†’    if (isNaN(r) || isNaN(g) || isNaN(b)) {
   237â†’      console.warn('analyzeColor: Invalid RGB values:', { r, g, b });
   238â†’      return null;
   239â†’    }
   240â†’
   241â†’    // Calculate brightness (luminance)
   242â†’    const brightness = 0.299 * r + 0.587 * g + 0.114 * b;
   243â†’
   244â†’    // Calculate contrast (simplified)
   245â†’    const max = Math.max(r, g, b);
   246â†’    const min = Math.min(r, g, b);
   247â†’    const contrast = (max - min) / (max + min + 0.001);
   248â†’
   249â†’    // Calculate dominant hue
   250â†’    const hue = rgbToHue(r, g, b);
   251â†’
   252â†’    return {
   253â†’      averageColor: `rgb(${Math.round(r * 255)}, ${Math.round(g * 255)}, ${Math.round(b * 255)})`,
   254â†’      brightness,
   255â†’      contrast,
   256â†’      dominantHue: hue,
   257â†’    };
   258â†’  } catch (error) {
   259â†’    console.warn('analyzeColor: Error processing color:', error);
   260â†’    // Return a safe default
   261â†’    return {
   262â†’      averageColor: 'rgb(128, 128, 128)',
   263â†’      brightness: 0.5,
   264â†’      contrast: 0.5,
   265â†’      dominantHue: 0,
   266â†’    };
   267â†’  }
   268â†’}
   269â†’
   270â†’// Helper function to convert RGB to HSL hue
   271â†’function rgbToHue(r: number, g: number, b: number): number {
   272â†’  const max = Math.max(r, g, b);
   273â†’  const min = Math.min(r, g, b);
   274â†’  const delta = max - min;
   275â†’
   276â†’  if (delta === 0) return 0;
   277â†’
   278â†’  let hue = 0;
   279â†’  if (max === r) {
   280â†’    hue = ((g - b) / delta) % 6;
   281â†’  } else if (max === g) {
   282â†’    hue = (b - r) / delta + 2;
   283â†’  } else {
   284â†’    hue = (r - g) / delta + 4;
   285â†’  }
   286â†’
   287â†’  return Math.round(hue * 60);
   288â†’}
   289â†’
```

   224â†’        onClick={handleClick}
   225â†’        {...props}
   226â†’      >
   227â†’        {/* Loading state overlay */}
   228â†’        {loading && (
   229â†’          <div
   230â†’            className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center bg-current/10 rounded-xl"
   231â†’            aria-hidden="true"
   232â†’          >
   233â†’            <div
   234â†’              className={cn(
   235â†’                'animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-current border-t-transparent',
   236â†’                iconSizeClasses[size]
   237â†’              )}
   238â†’            />
   239â†’          </div>
   240â†’        )}
   241â†’
   242â†’        <div
   243â†’          className={cn(
   244â†’            'flex items-center justify-center gap-2',
   245â†’            loading && 'opacity-0'
   246â†’          )}
   247â†’        >
   248â†’          {leftIcon && (
   249â†’            <span
   250â†’              className={cn('flex-shrink-0', iconSizeClasses[size])}
   251â†’              aria-hidden="true"
   252â†’            >
   253â†’              {leftIcon}
   254â†’            </span>
   255â†’          )}
   256â†’          <span className="truncate">{children}</span>
   257â†’          {rightIcon && (
   258â†’            <span
   259â†’              className={cn('flex-shrink-0', iconSizeClasses[size])}
   260â†’              aria-hidden="true"
   261â†’            >
   262â†’              {rightIcon}
   263â†’            </span>
   264â†’          )}
   265â†’        </div>
   266â†’      </button>
   267â†’    );
   268â†’  }
   269â†’);
   270â†’
   271â†’GlassButton.displayName = 'GlassButton';
   272â†’
   273â†’export { GlassButton };
   274â†’
```

## Current Liquid Glass Implementation

### **Core Files Structure**

The codebase has undergone a recent **Tailwind v4 migration** and contains a comprehensive liquid glass design system with the following key files:

### **1. Apple Liquid Glass Implementation**
- `/src/lib/apple-liquid-glass.ts` - Main Apple liquid glass hook and utilities
- `/src/styles/apple-liquid-glass.css` - Apple-specific liquid glass CSS classes
- `/src/styles/apple-liquid-authentic.css` - Authentic Apple glass materials

### **2. Core Design System**
- `/src/lib/liquid-glass-tokens.ts` - Comprehensive design tokens
- `/src/hooks/use-liquid-glass.tsx` - React hook for liquid glass effects
- `/src/styles/glass.css` - Main glass system CSS (1500+ lines)

### **3. Component System**
- `/src/components/glass-showcase/` - Showcase component demonstrating effects
- 50+ glass components in `/src/components/glass-*` directories
- `/src/components/glass-button/glass-button.tsx` - Example implementation

### **4. Utility & Configuration**
- `/src/lib/glass-utils.ts` - Utility functions and class generators
- `/src/lib/css-variables.ts` - Type-safe CSS variable system
- `/src/types/tailwind.d.ts` - TypeScript definitions

---

## **Implementation Features**

### **Apple-Authentic Effects**
- **Depth Layers**: 4 levels of glass depth with authentic Apple blur/saturation
- **Magnetic Hover**: Physics-based hover interactions
- **Specular Highlights**: Realistic glass reflection effects
- **Liquid Animations**: Smooth, spring-based transitions

### **Advanced Visual Effects**
- **Shimmer Effects**: Animated light reflections
- **Ripple Effects**: Click-based ripple animations
- **Holographic/Iridescent**: Advanced visual effects
- **Neon Glow**: Customizable glow effects
- **Crystal Effects**: Premium glass materials

### **Design System Integration**
- **CSS Custom Properties**: 100+ CSS variables for theming
- **Design Tokens**: Comprehensive token system
- **Responsive**: Mobile-first responsive design
- **Accessibility**: Focus rings, reduced motion support
- **Dark Mode**: Full dark theme support

---

## **Current State Analysis**

### **Recently Modified Files (from git status)**
- `glass-button.tsx` - Updated button component
- `glass-card.tsx` - Updated card component  
- `glass.css` - Main CSS file with all effects
- `glass-utils.ts` - Utility functions
- `liquid-glass-tokens.ts` - Design tokens

### **Recent Migration**
The codebase recently underwent a **Tailwind v4 migration**:
- Removed legacy `@tailwind` directives
- Updated to CSS layers (`@layer components`, `@layer utilities`)
- Enhanced TypeScript integration
- Improved CSS variable system

### **Available Glass Variants**

- `/src/styles/apple-liquid-glass.css` - Apple-specific liquid glass CSS classes
- `/src/styles/apple-liquid-authentic.css` - Authentic Apple glass materials

### **2. Core Design System**
- `/src/lib/liquid-glass-tokens.ts` - Comprehensive design tokens
- `/src/hooks/use-liquid-glass.tsx` - React hook for liquid glass effects
- `/src/styles/glass.css` - Main glass system CSS (1500+ lines)

### **3. Component System**
- `/src/components/glass-showcase/` - Showcase component demonstrating effects
- 50+ glass components in `/src/components/glass-*` directories
- `/src/components/glass-button/glass-button.tsx` - Example implementation

### **4. Utility & Configuration**
- `/src/lib/glass-utils.ts` - Utility functions and class generators
- `/src/lib/css-variables.ts` - Type-safe CSS variable system
- `/src/types/tailwind.d.ts` - TypeScript definitions

---

## **Implementation Features**

### **Apple-Authentic Effects**
- **Depth Layers**: 4 levels of glass depth with authentic Apple blur/saturation
- **Magnetic Hover**: Physics-based hover interactions
- **Specular Highlights**: Realistic glass reflection effects
- **Liquid Animations**: Smooth, spring-based transitions

### **Advanced Visual Effects**
- **Shimmer Effects**: Animated light reflections
- **Ripple Effects**: Click-based ripple animations
- **Holographic/Iridescent**: Advanced visual effects
- **Neon Glow**: Customizable glow effects
- **Crystal Effects**: Premium glass materials

### **Design System Integration**
- **CSS Custom Properties**: 100+ CSS variables for theming
- **Design Tokens**: Comprehensive token system
- **Responsive**: Mobile-first responsive design
- **Accessibility**: Focus rings, reduced motion support
- **Dark Mode**: Full dark theme support

---

## **Current State Analysis**

### **Recently Modified Files (from git status)**
- `glass-button.tsx` - Updated button component
- `glass-card.tsx` - Updated card component  
- `glass.css` - Main CSS file with all effects
- `glass-utils.ts` - Utility functions
- `liquid-glass-tokens.ts` - Design tokens

### **Recent Migration**
The codebase recently underwent a **Tailwind v4 migration**:
- Removed legacy `@tailwind` directives
- Updated to CSS layers (`@layer components`, `@layer utilities`)
- Enhanced TypeScript integration
- Improved CSS variable system

### **Available Glass Variants**
\```typescript
// From apple-liquid-glass.ts
APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS = {
  subtle: { blur: 12px, background: rgba(255,255,255,0.08) },
  medium: { blur: 20px, background: rgba(255,255,255,0.15) },
  strong: { blur: 32px, background: rgba(255,255,255,0.25) }
}

// From glass-utils.ts
glassVariants = {
  'apple-interactive': 'apple-glass apple-glass--depth-2 apple-glass--magnetic',
  'apple-shimmer': 'apple-glass apple-glass--depth-2 apple-glass--shimmer',
  'apple-ripple': 'apple-glass apple-glass--depth-2 apple-glass--ripple'
}
\```

## **Key Implementation Highlights**

### **1. Comprehensive CSS System**
The `/src/styles/glass.css` file contains 1500+ lines with:
- Apple system colors and materials
- Interactive states and animations
- Advanced effects (plasma, aurora, crystal, etc.)
- Accessibility and responsive support

### **2. Type-Safe Implementation**
- Full TypeScript support with custom type definitions
- Type-safe CSS variable access
- Enhanced IntelliSense for design tokens

### **3. Performance Optimized**
- GSAP-ready animations (`will-change`, `transform: translateZ(0)`)
- Efficient backdrop filters
- Reduced motion support

### **4. Modern Component Architecture**
- React hooks for glass effects
- Configurable magnetic hover
- Content-aware adaptations
- Haptic feedback support

The implementation represents a **production-ready, comprehensive liquid glass design system** that authentically replicates Apple's 2025+ design language with advanced visual effects and interactions.

Apple Liquid Glass UI (2025)
----------------------------
Forked from https://codepen.io/wprod/details/raVpwJL

        <feTurbulence type="fractalNoise" baseFrequency="0.008 0.008" numOctaves="2" seed="92" result="noise" />
        <feGaussianBlur in="noise" stdDeviation="2" result="blurred" />
        <feDisplacementMap in="SourceGraphic" in2="blurred" scale="70" xChannelSelector="R" yChannelSelector="G" />
      </filter>

script.js

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('.menu li');
    
    menuItems.forEach(item => {
        item.addEventListener('click', () => {
            menuItems.forEach(i => i.classList.remove('active'));
            item.classList.add('active');
            
            const icon = item.querySelector('i');
            icon.style.transform = 'scale(1.2)';
            setTimeout(() => {
                icon.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
            }, 200);
        });
    });
    
    menuItems.forEach(item => {
        item.addEventListener('mouseenter', (e) => {
            const highlight = document.createElement('div');
            highlight.classList.add('highlight');
            highlight.style.position = 'absolute';
            highlight.style.top = '0';
            highlight.style.left = '0';
            highlight.style.width = '100%';
            highlight.style.height = '100%';
            highlight.style.borderRadius = '16px';
            highlight.style.background = 'radial-gradient(circle at ' + (e.offsetX) + 'px ' + (e.offsetY) + 'px, rgba(255,255,255,0.2) 0%, rgba(255,255,255,0) 70%)';
            highlight.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
            
            item.appendChild(highlight);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                highlight.style.opacity = '0';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    item.removeChild(highlight);
                }, 300);
            }, 500);
        });
    });
    
    const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.card');
    cards.forEach(card => {
        card.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
            const rect = card.getBoundingClientRect();
            const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
            const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
            
            const rotateY = (x / rect.width - 0.5) * 10;
            const rotateX = (y / rect.height - 0.5) * -10;
            
            card.style.transform = `perspective(1000px) rotateX(${rotateX}deg) rotateY(${rotateY}deg) scale(1.05)`;
        });
        
        card.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
            card.style.transform = 'translateY(0) scale(1)';
            card.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s ease';
        });
    });
});

Based on my search results, I can provide you with comprehensive information about Tailwind CSS v4's new features in 2025, particularly regarding CSS layers, utilities, and components.

## Tailwind CSS v4 New Features in 2025

### CSS Layers Architecture
Tailwind CSS v4 is built on cutting-edge CSS features like cascade layers. Tailwind uses CSS layers so you don't have to worry about specificity issues, with the structure: @layer theme, base, components, utilities. The framework now uses real @layer rules, which solves a ton of specificity problems.

### Performance Improvements
Tailwind CSS v4.0 is a ground-up rewrite of the framework, with full rebuilds being over 3.5x faster, and incremental builds being over 8x faster. The most remarkable boost comes from incremental builds that don't require compiling new CSSâ€”these are now over 100x faster, running in mere microseconds.

### New Utilities and Features
Tailwind v4 includes even more new utilities and variants â€” including support for color-scheme, field-sizing, complex shadows, inert, and more. Specific new utilities include:

- inset-shadow-* & inset-ring-* Utilities â€“ Stack up to four layers of box shadows on a single element
- New Field Sizing Utilities â€“ Auto-resizing areas without writing a single line of JavaScript
- Color Scheme Utilities â€“ Remove unwanted light scrollbars in dark mode
- Font Stretch Utilities â€“ Adjust variable fonts that support different widths
- New inert Variant â€“ Style non-interactive elements marked with the inert attribute
- New nth-* Variants â€“ Advanced styling for targeting specific elements dynamically
- New in-* Variant â€“ Similar to group-*, but without requiring a .group wrapper

### CSS-First Configuration
The new CSS-first configuration lets you do just about everything you could do in your tailwind.config.js file, including configuring your design tokens, defining custom utilities and variants. CSS theme variables expose all of your design tokens as native CSS variables so you can access them anywhere.

### Modern CSS Features
Tailwind v4 uses @property to define internal custom properties with proper types and constraints, making it possible to do things like transition background gradients, and uses color-mix for opacity modifiers. Container queries are now supported in core, with new @min-* and @max-* variants to support container query ranges.

### Simplified Installation
Tailwind v4 features simplified installation with fewer dependencies, zero configuration, and just a single line of code in your CSS file. It includes a first-party Vite plugin for tight integration and automatic content detection where all template files are discovered automatically.

### Release Information
The long-awaited release of Tailwind CSS 4.0 on January 22, 2025, allows developers to explore its groundbreaking new features. This version has a complete architectural overhaul with the new Oxide engine, which boosts build speeds and reduces bundle sizes.

This represents a significant evolution in Tailwind CSS, focusing on performance, modern CSS capabilities, and developer experience improvements while maintaining the utility-first approach that made the framework popular.

Links: [{"title":"React Design Patterns and Best Practices for 2025","url":"https://www.telerik.com/blogs/react-design-patterns-best-practices"},{"title":"React v19 â€“ React","url":"https://react.dev/blog/2024/12/05/react-19"},{"title":"React 19 : New Features and Updates - GeeksforGeeks","url":"https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/react-19-new-features-and-updates/"},{"title":"React Architecture Pattern and Best Practices in 2025 - GeeksforGeeks","url":"https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/react-architecture-pattern-and-best-practices/"},{"title":"Whatâ€™s new in React 19 - Vercel","url":"https://vercel.com/blog/whats-new-in-react-19"},{"title":"Everything on React 19 New Features and Updates","url":"https://www.kellton.com/kellton-tech-blog/react-19-latest-features-and-updates"},{"title":"React 19 Features & Updates (2025): Whatâ€™s New & Why It Matters - WEQ","url":"https://weqtechnologies.com/react-19-features-updates-2025-whats-new-why-it-matters/"},{"title":"New React 19 Features You Should Know â€“ Explained with Code Examples","url":"https://www.freecodecamp.org/news/new-react-19-features-you-should-know-with-code-examples/"},{"title":"React 19 Upgrade Guide â€“ React","url":"https://react.dev/blog/2024/04/25/react-19-upgrade-guide"},{"title":"React 19 â€“ New Hooks Explained with Examples","url":"https://www.freecodecamp.org/news/react-19-new-hooks-explained-with-examples/"}]

Here are the key React 19 features, hooks, patterns, and component architecture updates for 2025:

## New React 19 Hooks

React 19 introduced several new hooks, which include useActionState, useFormStatus, useOptimistic and the new use API. These hooks provide elegant solutions for common development tasks:

### useActionState
This hook simplifies managing form states and form submissions. Using Actions, it captures form input data, handles validation, and error states, reducing the need for custom state management logic. The useActionState hook also exposes a pending state that can show a loading indicator while the action is being executed.

### useFormStatus
This hook manages the status of the last form submission, and it must be called from inside a component that is also inside a form. React 19 introduces useFormStatus, a hook that simplifies access to parent form information within child components. This is particularly valuable in design systems where components need to interact with form state without excessive prop drilling.

### useOptimistic
The useOptimistic hook in React 19 facilitates optimistic UI updates during asynchronous data mutations. This pattern allows immediate display of expected outcomes while data updates are in progress. Actions support the new useOptimistic hook so you can show users instant feedback while the requests are submitting.

### use API
In React 19 we're introducing a new API to read resources in render: use. The use function offers first-class support for promises and context during rendering. Unlike other React Hooks, use can be called within loops, conditional statements, and early returns.

## Actions - A New Pattern

Actions are a new concept in React 19, simplify the process of handling form submissions and integrating with React's concurrent features. React 19 introduces Actions. These functions replace using event handlers and integrate with React transitions and concurrent features.

Actions automatically manage submitting data for you: Pending state: Actions provide a pending state that starts at the beginning of a request and automatically resets when the final state update is committed. Optimistic updates: Actions support the new useOptimistic hook so you can show users instant feedback while the requests are submitting. Error handling: Actions provide error handling so you can display Error Boundaries when a request fails, and revert optimistic updates to their original value automatically.

## Component Architecture Improvements

### Server Components
Server Components are one of the biggest changes to React since its initial release 10 years ago. They act as a foundation for React 19's new features, improving: Initial page load times. By rendering components on the server, they reduce the amount of JavaScript sent to the client, resulting in faster initial loads.

### Ref Handling Improvements
React 19 introduces a notable enhancement for refs: functional components can now directly accept refs as props. This advancement often eliminates the need for the forwardRef higher-order component.

## Modern React Patterns for 2025

### Function Components Standard
Function components have become the de facto standard for React development, replacing class components for practically all use cases. This shift reflects React's move toward a more functional programming paradigm, emphasizing simplicity and composability.

### TypeScript Integration
React 19 improves TypeScript support by offering better type inference, especially with new hooks and APIs. The enhanced TypeScript definitions help developers catch errors early in development and write more robust, type-safe code.

### Automatic Optimizations
With the React Compiler in React 19, memoization is handled automatically, so you no longer need to use hooks like useMemo or useCallback for performance optimization.

## Framework Ecosystem for 2025

The modern React ecosystem has evolved significantly, with frameworks playing a critical role in elevating developer experience and application performance. In 2025, three solutions often stand out in the React development landscape: Next.js, Remix and Vite.

## Performance Enhancements

### Concurrent Features
Concurrent rendering is one of the most significant features that comes with React framework. It helps React developers unlock maximum performance for React applications, along with improved responsiveness. Concurrent rendering prioritizes the critical updates and holds the less important tasks to drive seamless user interactions during heavy rendering workloads.

### Automatic Batching
React 19 has very soon become a popular choice of front-end JS development because of its powerful feature known as "automatic batching." As the name indicates, automatic batching is a smart mechanism within React engineered particularly for performance optimization.

These updates represent a significant evolution in React development patterns, focusing on improved developer experience, better performance, and more elegant solutions for common development challenges.

1â†’/**
     2â†’ * Apple Liquid Glass Effects
     3â†’ * Authentic Apple-style liquid glass implementation with physics-based interactions
     4â†’ */
     5â†’
     6â†’import { useRef, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
     7â†’
     8â†’export interface AppleLiquidGlassOptions {
     9â†’  intensity?: 'subtle' | 'medium' | 'strong';
    10â†’  magneticStrength?: number;
    11â†’  liquidFlow?: boolean;
    12â†’  enableHaptics?: boolean;
    13â†’}
    14â†’
    15â†’export const APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS = {
    16â†’  subtle: {
    17â†’    background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.08)',
    18â†’    backdropFilter: 'blur(12px) saturate(150%)',
    19â†’    border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.6)',
    20â†’    borderRadius: '24px',
    21â†’  },
    22â†’  medium: {
    23â†’    background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15)',
    24â†’    backdropFilter: 'blur(20px) saturate(180%)',
    25â†’    border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)',
    26â†’    borderRadius: '32px',
    27â†’  },
    28â†’  strong: {
    29â†’    background: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.25)',
    30â†’    backdropFilter: 'blur(32px) saturate(200%)',
    31â†’    border: '1px solid rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9)',
    32â†’    borderRadius: '40px',
    33â†’  },
    34â†’} as const;
    35â†’
    36â†’export const APPLE_LIQUID_SHADOWS = {
    37â†’  subtle: '0 4px 16px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.1), inset 0 2px 10px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.2)',
    38â†’  medium: '0 8px 32px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.2), inset 0 4px 20px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)',
    39â†’  strong: '0 16px 48px rgba(31, 38, 135, 0.3), inset 0 8px 32px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.4)',
    40â†’} as const;
    41â†’
    42â†’export const APPLE_LIQUID_AFTER_EFFECTS = {
    43â†’  subtle: {
    44â†’    boxShadow: 'inset -6px -4px 0px -7px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8), inset 0px -5px 0px -4px rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)',
    45â†’    filter: 'blur(0.5px) drop-shadow(6px 2px 4px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2)) brightness(110%)',
    46â†’  },
    47â†’  medium: {
    48â†’    boxShadow: 'inset -10px -8px 0px -11px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1), inset 0px -9px 0px -8px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1)',
    49â†’    filter: 'blur(1px) drop-shadow(10px 4px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)) brightness(115%)',
    50â†’  },
    51â†’  strong: {
    52â†’    boxShadow: 'inset -14px -12px 0px -15px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1), inset 0px -13px 0px -12px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1)',
    53â†’    filter: 'blur(1.5px) drop-shadow(14px 6px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4)) brightness(120%)',
    54â†’  },
    55â†’} as const;
    56â†’
    57â†’/**
    58â†’ * Hook for Apple liquid glass magnetic hover effect
    59â†’ */
    60â†’export function useAppleLiquidGlass(options: AppleLiquidGlassOptions = {}) {
    61â†’  const elementRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);
    62â†’  const {
    63â†’    intensity = 'medium',
    64â†’    magneticStrength = 0.3,
    65â†’    liquidFlow = true,
    66â†’    enableHaptics = false,
    67â†’  } = options;
    68â†’
    69â†’  const handleMouseMove = useCallback((e: MouseEvent) => {
    70â†’    if (!elementRef.current) return;
    71â†’
    72â†’    const rect = elementRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();
    73â†’    const centerX = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
    74â†’    const centerY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
    75â†’    
    76â†’    const deltaX = (e.clientX - centerX) * magneticStrength;
    77â†’    const deltaY = (e.clientY - centerY) * magneticStrength;
    78â†’
    79â†’    elementRef.current.style.transform = `translate(${deltaX}px, ${deltaY}px) translateZ(0)`;
    80â†’    
    81â†’    if (liquidFlow) {
    82â†’      const afterElement = elementRef.current.querySelector('::after') as HTMLElement;
    83â†’      if (afterElement) {
    84â†’        afterElement.style.transform = `translate(${-deltaX * 0.5}px, ${-deltaY * 0.5}px)`;
    85â†’      }
    86â†’    }
    87â†’  }, [magneticStrength, liquidFlow]);
    88â†’
    89â†’  const handleMouseLeave = useCallback(() => {
    90â†’    if (!elementRef.current) return;
    91â†’    
    92â†’    elementRef.current.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px) translateZ(0)';
    93â†’    elementRef.current.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
    94â†’    
    95â†’    setTimeout(() => {
    96â†’      if (elementRef.current) {
    97â†’        elementRef.current.style.transition = '';
    98â†’      }
    99â†’    }, 500);
   100â†’
   101â†’    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   102â†’      navigator.vibrate(10);
   103â†’    }
   104â†’  }, [enableHaptics]);
   105â†’
   106â†’  const handleMouseEnter = useCallback(() => {
   107â†’    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   108â†’      navigator.vibrate(5);
   109â†’    }
   110â†’  }, [enableHaptics]);
   111â†’
   112â†’  useEffect(() => {
   113â†’    const element = elementRef.current;
   114â†’    if (!element) return;
   115â†’
   116â†’    element.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   117â†’    element.addEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   118â†’    element.addEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   119â†’
   120â†’    return () => {
   121â†’      element.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   122â†’      element.removeEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   123â†’      element.removeEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   124â†’    };
   125â†’  }, [handleMouseMove, handleMouseLeave, handleMouseEnter]);
   126â†’
   127â†’  return {
   128â†’    ref: elementRef,
   129â†’    variant: APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS[intensity],
   130â†’    shadow: APPLE_LIQUID_SHADOWS[intensity],
   131â†’    afterEffect: APPLE_LIQUID_AFTER_EFFECTS[intensity],
   132â†’  };
   133â†’}
   134â†’
   135â†’/**
   136â†’ * Generate Apple liquid glass CSS classes - Tailwind v4 Compatible
   137â†’ */
   138â†’export function getAppleLiquidGlassClass(
   139â†’  intensity: keyof typeof APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS = 'medium',
   140â†’  interactive = true
   141â†’): string {
   142â†’  const baseClass = 'apple-liquid-glass';
   143â†’  const intensityClass = intensity !== 'medium' ? `apple-liquid-glass--${intensity}` : '';
   144â†’  const interactiveClass = interactive ? 'apple-liquid-glass--interactive' : '';
   145â†’  
   146â†’  return [baseClass, intensityClass, interactiveClass].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
   147â†’}
   148â†’
   149â†’/**
   150â†’ * Apple liquid glass animation presets
   151â†’ */
   152â†’export const APPLE_LIQUID_ANIMATIONS = {
   153â†’  hover: {
   154â†’    transform: 'translateY(-2px)',
   155â†’    transition: 'all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   156â†’  },
   157â†’  active: {
   158â†’    transform: 'translateY(0px) scale(0.98)',
   159â†’    transition: 'all 0.15s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   160â†’  },
   161â†’  focus: {
   162â†’    boxShadow: '0 0 0 3px rgba(0, 122, 255, 0.3)',
   163â†’    transition: 'box-shadow 0.2s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   164â†’  },
   165â†’} as const;

    75â†’export function useAppleLiquidGlass(options: AppleLiquidGlassOptions = {}) {
    76â†’  const elementRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);
    77â†’  const {
    78â†’    intensity = 'medium',
    79â†’    magneticStrength = 0.3,
    80â†’    liquidFlow = true,
    81â†’    enableHaptics = false,
    82â†’    multiLayer = false,
    83â†’    animated = false,
    84â†’    distortionEffect = false,
    85â†’  } = options;
    86â†’
    87â†’  const handleMouseMove = useCallback((e: MouseEvent) => {
    88â†’    if (!elementRef.current) return;
    89â†’
    90â†’    // Use startTransition for smooth animations
    91â†’    startTransition(() => {
    92â†’      const rect = elementRef.current!.getBoundingClientRect();
    93â†’      const centerX = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
    94â†’      const centerY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
    95â†’      
    96â†’      const deltaX = (e.clientX - centerX) * magneticStrength;
    97â†’      const deltaY = (e.clientY - centerY) * magneticStrength;
    98â†’
    99â†’      elementRef.current!.style.transform = `translate(${deltaX}px, ${deltaY}px) translateZ(0)`;
   100â†’      
   101â†’      if (liquidFlow && multiLayer) {
   102â†’        // Enhanced liquid flow for multi-layer structure
   103â†’        const glassFilter = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-filter') as HTMLElement;
   104â†’        const glassOverlay = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-overlay') as HTMLElement;
   105â†’        
   106â†’        if (glassFilter) {
   107â†’          glassFilter.style.transform = `translate(${-deltaX * 0.2}px, ${-deltaY * 0.2}px)`;
   108â†’        }
   109â†’        
   110â†’        if (glassOverlay) {
   111â†’          glassOverlay.style.transform = `translate(${-deltaX * 0.1}px, ${-deltaY * 0.1}px)`;
   112â†’        }
   113â†’      }
   114â†’    });
   115â†’  }, [magneticStrength, liquidFlow, multiLayer]);
   116â†’
   117â†’  const handleMouseLeave = useCallback(() => {
   118â†’    if (!elementRef.current) return;
   119â†’    
   120â†’    startTransition(() => {
   121â†’      elementRef.current!.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px) translateZ(0)';
   122â†’      elementRef.current!.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   123â†’      
   124â†’      if (multiLayer) {
   125â†’        const glassFilter = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-filter') as HTMLElement;
   126â†’        const glassOverlay = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-overlay') as HTMLElement;
   127â†’        
   128â†’        if (glassFilter) {
   129â†’          glassFilter.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px)';
   130â†’          glassFilter.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   131â†’        }
   132â†’        
   133â†’        if (glassOverlay) {
   134â†’          glassOverlay.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px)';
   135â†’          glassOverlay.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   136â†’        }
   137â†’      }
   138â†’      
   139â†’      setTimeout(() => {
   140â†’        if (elementRef.current) {

   156â†’    }
   157â†’  }, [enableHaptics, multiLayer]);
   158â†’

   160â†’    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   161â†’      navigator.vibrate(5);
   162â†’    }
   163â†’  }, [enableHaptics]);

   166â†’    const element = elementRef.current;
   167â†’    if (!element) return;
   168â†’
   169â†’    element.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   170â†’    element.addEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   171â†’    element.addEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   172â†’
   173â†’    return () => {
   174â†’      element.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   175â†’      element.removeEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   176â†’      element.removeEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   177â†’    };
   178â†’  }, [handleMouseMove, handleMouseLeave, handleMouseEnter]);
   179â†’
   180â†’  return {
   181â†’    ref: elementRef,
   182â†’    variant: APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS[intensity],
   183â†’    shadow: APPLE_LIQUID_SHADOWS[intensity],

   196â†’  intensity: keyof typeof APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS = 'medium',
   197â†’  options: {
   198â†’    interactive?: boolean;
   199â†’    magnetic?: boolean;
   200â†’    animated?: boolean;

   205â†’  
   206â†’  const baseClass = 'apple-liquid-glass';
   207â†’  const intensityClass = intensity !== 'medium' ? `apple-liquid-glass--${intensity}` : '';
   208â†’  const interactiveClass = interactive ? 'apple-liquid-glass--interactive' : '';
   209â†’  const magneticClass = magnetic ? 'apple-liquid-glass--magnetic' : '';
   210â†’  const animatedClass = animated ? 'apple-liquid-glass--animated' : '';
   211â†’  
   212â†’  return [baseClass, intensityClass, interactiveClass, magneticClass, animatedClass].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
   213â†’}

/**
 * Apple Liquid Glass SVG Filters Component
 * Provides SVG filter definitions for authentic liquid glass distortion effects
 */

import { memo } from 'react';

export interface LiquidGlassSvgFiltersProps {
  className?: string;
}

/**
 * SVG filter definitions for liquid glass effects
 * Based on patterns from Apple's authentic liquid glass implementations
 */
export const LiquidGlassSvgFilters = memo(function LiquidGlassSvgFilters({
  className = 'apple-liquid-svg-defs',
}: LiquidGlassSvgFiltersProps) {
  return (
    <svg 
      className={className}
      style={{ 
        position: 'absolute', 
        width: 0, 
        height: 0, 
        overflow: 'hidden' 
      }}
      aria-hidden="true"
    >
      <defs>
        {/* Liquid Lens Filter - Creates distortion effect */}
        <filter 
          id="liquid-lens" 
          x="-50%" 
          y="-50%" 
          width="200%" 
          height="200%"
        >
          <feImage 
            x="0" 
            y="0" 
            result="normalMap" 
            xlinkHref="data:image/svg+xml;utf8,<svg xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg' width='300' height='300'><radialGradient id='nmap' cx='50%' cy='50%' r='50%'><stop offset='0%' stop-color='rgb(128,128,255)'/><stop offset='100%' stop-color='rgb(255,255,255)'/></radialGradient><rect width='100%' height='100%' fill='url(%23nmap)'/></svg>" 
          />
          <feDisplacementMap 
            in="SourceGraphic" 
            in2="normalMap" 
            scale="60" 
            xChannelSelector="R" 
            yChannelSelector="G" 
            result="displaced" 
          />
          <feMerge>
            <feMergeNode in="displaced" />
          </feMerge>
        </filter>
        
        {/* Liquid Distortion Filter - Creates turbulence effect */}
        <filter 
          id="liquid-distortion" 
          x="0%" 
          y="0%" 
          width="100%" 
          height="100%"
        >
          <feTurbulence 
            type="fractalNoise" 
            baseFrequency="0.008 0.008" 
            numOctaves="2" 
            seed="92" 
            result="noise" 
          />
          <feGaussianBlur 
            in="noise" 
            stdDeviation="2" 
            result="blurred" 
          />
          <feDisplacementMap 
            in="SourceGraphic" 
            in2="blurred" 
            scale="70" 
            xChannelSelector="R" 
            yChannelSelector="G" 
          />
        </filter>
        
        {/* Subtle Liquid Effect - Light distortion */}
        <filter 
          id="liquid-subtle" 
          x="0%" 
          y="0%" 
          width="100%" 
          height="100%"
        >
          <feTurbulence 
            type="fractalNoise" 
            baseFrequency="0.004 0.004" 
            numOctaves="1" 
            seed="42" 
            result="noise" 
          />
          <feGaussianBlur 
            in="noise" 
            stdDeviation="1" 
            result="blurred" 
          />
          <feDisplacementMap 
            in="SourceGraphic" 
            in2="blurred" 
            scale="30" 
            xChannelSelector="R" 
            yChannelSelector="G" 
          />
        </filter>
        
        {/* Strong Liquid Effect - Heavy distortion */}
        <filter 
          id="liquid-strong" 
          x="0%" 
          y="0%" 
          width="100%" 
          height="100%"
        >
          <feTurbulence 
            type="fractalNoise" 
            baseFrequency="0.012 0.012" 
            numOctaves="3" 
            seed="123" 
            result="noise" 
          />
          <feGaussianBlur 
            in="noise" 
            stdDeviation="3" 
            result="blurred" 
          />
          <feDisplacementMap 
            in="SourceGraphic" 
            in2="blurred" 
            scale="100" 
            xChannelSelector="R" 
            yChannelSelector="G" 
          />
        </filter>
        
        {/* Liquid Glow Filter - Adds luminous effect */}
        <filter 
          id="liquid-glow" 
          x="-50%" 
          y="-50%" 
          width="200%" 
          height="200%"
        >
          <feGaussianBlur 
            stdDeviation="3" 
            result="coloredBlur"
          />
          <feMerge>
            <feMergeNode in="coloredBlur"/>
            <feMergeNode in="SourceGraphic"/>
          </feMerge>
        </filter>
        
        {/* Liquid Shimmer Filter - Animated highlight effect */}
        <filter 
          id="liquid-shimmer" 
          x="-50%" 
          y="-50%" 
          width="200%" 
          height="200%"
        >
          <feGaussianBlur 
            in="SourceGraphic" 
            stdDeviation="1" 
            result="blur"
          />
          <feSpecularLighting 
            in="blur" 
            specularConstant="1.5" 
            specularExponent="20" 
            lighting-color="white" 
            result="specOut"
          >
            <fePointLight x="50" y="50" z="100"/>
          </feSpecularLighting>
          <feComposite 
            in="specOut" 
            in2="SourceAlpha" 
            operator="in" 
            result="specOut2"
          />
          <feComposite 
            in="SourceGraphic" 
            in2="specOut2" 
            operator="arithmetic" 
            k1="0" 
            k2="1" 
            k3="1" 
            k4="0"
          />
        </filter>
      </defs>
    </svg>
  );
});

export default LiquidGlassSvgFilters;

Now let me create a comprehensive Apple Liquid Glass component that uses the multi-layer structure:

_**Agent (claude-sonnet-4-20250514)**_

Tool use: **Write**

```tsx
/**
 * Apple Liquid Glass Component
 * Authentic Apple-style liquid glass with multi-layer structure
 * Based on patterns from GitHub gists and enhanced with React 19 features
 */

import { forwardRef, HTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { 
  useAppleLiquidGlass, 
  getAppleLiquidGlassClass, 
  createGlassLayers,
  AppleLiquidGlassProps 
} from '../lib/apple-liquid-glass';

export interface AppleLiquidGlassComponentProps 
  extends Omit<HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement>, 'className'>, AppleLiquidGlassProps {
  as?: keyof JSX.IntrinsicElements;
  contentClassName?: string;
}

/**
 * Apple Liquid Glass Component with multi-layer structure
 * Supports both legacy single-layer and new multi-layer implementations
 */
export const AppleLiquidGlass = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, AppleLiquidGlassComponentProps>(
  function AppleLiquidGlass({
    children,
    className = '',
    contentClassName = '',
    multiLayer = true,
    intensity = 'medium',
    interactive = true,
    magnetic = false,
    animated = false,
    as: Component = 'div',
    ...props
  }, ref) {
    const { ref: glassRef } = useAppleLiquidGlass({
      intensity,
      magneticStrength: magnetic ? 0.3 : 0,
      liquidFlow: true,
      enableHaptics: false,
      multiLayer,
      animated,
      distortionEffect: true,
    });

    const glassClassName = getAppleLiquidGlassClass(intensity, {
      interactive,
      magnetic,
      animated,
      multiLayer,
    });

    // Combine refs - React 19 style (no forwardRef needed in some cases)
    const combinedRef = (element: HTMLDivElement | null) => {
      if (typeof ref === 'function') {
        ref(element);
      } else if (ref) {
        ref.current = element;
      }
      
      if (glassRef) {
        (glassRef as any).current = element;
      }
    };

    const combinedClassName = `${glassClassName} ${className}`.trim();

    if (multiLayer) {
      return (
        <Component
          ref={combinedRef}
          className={combinedClassName}
          {...props}
        >
          {createGlassLayers(children, contentClassName)}
        </Component>
      );
    }

    // Legacy single-layer implementation
    return (
      <Component
        ref={combinedRef}
        className={combinedClassName}
        {...props}
      >
        {children}
      </Component>
    );
  }
);

/**
 * Apple Liquid Glass Card Component
 * Pre-configured glass card with common patterns
 */
export const AppleLiquidGlassCard = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, AppleLiquidGlassComponentProps>(
  function AppleLiquidGlassCard({
    className = '',
    contentClassName = 'gap-4',
    ...props
  }, ref) {
    return (
      <AppleLiquidGlass
        ref={ref}
        className={`p-6 ${className}`}
        contentClassName={contentClassName}
        {...props}
      />
    );
  }
);

/**
 * Apple Liquid Glass Button Component
 * Pre-configured glass button with interactive states
 */
export const AppleLiquidGlassButton = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, 
  Omit<AppleLiquidGlassComponentProps, 'as'> & { 
    variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'ghost';
    size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  }
>(
  function AppleLiquidGlassButton({
    className = '',
    contentClassName = 'justify-center',
    variant = 'primary',
    size = 'md',
    interactive = true,
    magnetic = true,
    ...props
  }, ref) {
    const sizeClasses = {
      sm: 'px-4 py-2 text-sm',
      md: 'px-6 py-3 text-base',
      lg: 'px-8 py-4 text-lg',
    };

    const variantClasses = {
      primary: 'font-semibold',
      secondary: 'font-medium',
      ghost: 'font-normal',
    };

    const buttonClassName = `
      ${sizeClasses[size]} 
      ${variantClasses[variant]} 
      cursor-pointer select-none
      ${className}
    `.trim();

    return (
      <AppleLiquidGlass
        ref={ref}
        as="button"
        className={buttonClassName}
        contentClassName={contentClassName}
        interactive={interactive}
        magnetic={magnetic}
        {...props}
      />
    );
  }
);

/**
 * Apple Liquid Glass Navigation Component
 * Pre-configured glass navigation with sidebar patterns
 */
export const AppleLiquidGlassNav = forwardRef<HTMLNavElement, 
  Omit<AppleLiquidGlassComponentProps, 'as'>
>(
  function AppleLiquidGlassNav({
    className = '',
    contentClassName = 'flex items-center',
    intensity = 'subtle',
    ...props
  }, ref) {
    return (
      <AppleLiquidGlass
        ref={ref}
        as="nav"
        className={className}
        contentClassName={contentClassName}
        intensity={intensity}
        {...props}
      />
    );
  }
);

export default AppleLiquidGlass;
```

/**
 * Apple Liquid Glass Showcase Page
 * Demonstrates all the new liquid glass effects and patterns
 * Based on authentic Apple design language from GitHub gists
 */

import { useState } from 'react';
import { 
  AppleLiquidGlass, 
  AppleLiquidGlassCard, 
  AppleLiquidGlassButton, 
  AppleLiquidGlassNav 
} from '../components/apple-liquid-glass';
import LiquidGlassSvgFilters from '../components/liquid-glass-svg-filters';

export default function AppleLiquidGlassShowcase() {
  const [selectedIntensity, setSelectedIntensity] = useState<'subtle' | 'medium' | 'strong'>('medium');
  const [enabledEffects, setEnabledEffects] = useState({
    magnetic: true,
    animated: false,
    multiLayer: true,
  });

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-600 via-purple-700 to-indigo-800 p-8">
      {/* Include SVG filters */}
      <LiquidGlassSvgFilters />
      
      {/* Background pattern */}
      <div 
        className="fixed inset-0 pointer-events-none"
        style={{
          backgroundImage: `
            radial-gradient(circle at 20% 50%, rgba(120, 119, 198, 0.3) 0%, transparent 50%),
            radial-gradient(circle at 80% 20%, rgba(255, 119, 198, 0.3) 0%, transparent 50%),
            radial-gradient(circle at 40% 80%, rgba(120, 219, 255, 0.3) 0%, transparent 50%)
          `,
        }}
      />

      <div className="relative z-10 max-w-6xl mx-auto">
        {/* Header */}
        <AppleLiquidGlassCard 
          className="mb-8 text-center"
          intensity="subtle"
          animated={true}
        >
          <h1 className="text-4xl font-bold text-white mb-4">
            Apple Liquid Glass Showcase
          </h1>
          <p className="text-lg text-white/80">
            Authentic Apple 2025 liquid glass design language
          </p>
        </AppleLiquidGlassCard>

        {/* Controls */}
        <AppleLiquidGlassCard className="mb-8">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-white mb-4">
            Effect Controls
          </h2>
          
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {/* Intensity Control */}
            <div>
              <label className="block text-white text-sm font-medium mb-2">
                Intensity
              </label>
              <div className="flex gap-2">
                {(['subtle', 'medium', 'strong'] as const).map((intensity) => (
                  <AppleLiquidGlassButton
                    key={intensity}
                    size="sm"
                    intensity={selectedIntensity === intensity ? 'strong' : 'subtle'}
                    onClick={() => setSelectedIntensity(intensity)}
                    className={selectedIntensity === intensity ? 'ring-2 ring-white/50' : ''}
                  >
                    {intensity.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + intensity.slice(1)}
                  </AppleLiquidGlassButton>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Effect Toggles */}
            <div>
              <label className="block text-white text-sm font-medium mb-2">
                Effects
              </label>
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                {Object.entries(enabledEffects).map(([effect, enabled]) => (
                  <AppleLiquidGlassButton
                    key={effect}
                    size="sm"
                    intensity={enabled ? 'strong' : 'subtle'}
                    onClick={() => setEnabledEffects(prev => ({
                      ...prev,
                      [effect]: !prev[effect as keyof typeof prev]
                    }))}
                    className={enabled ? 'ring-2 ring-white/50' : ''}
                  >
                    {effect.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + effect.slice(1)}
                  </AppleLiquidGlassButton>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </AppleLiquidGlassCard>

        {/* Glass Components Grid */}

            intensity={selectedIntensity}
            magnetic={enabledEffects.magnetic}
            animated={enabledEffects.animated}
            multiLayer={enabledEffects.multiLayer}
          >
            <div className="text-center">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-4">ğŸµ</div>

              </h3>

                Apple Music interface with liquid glass effects
              </p>
            </div>
          </AppleLiquidGlassCard>

          {/* Interactive Glass Card */}
          <AppleLiquidGlassCard
            intensity={selectedIntensity}
            magnetic={enabledEffects.magnetic}

            multiLayer={enabledEffects.multiLayer}
            interactive={true}
          >
            <div className="text-center">
              <div className="text-4xl mb-4">ğŸ“±</div>

            <div className="text-center">

    31â†’ * - Multiple variants (primary, secondary, tertiary, ghost, destructive)

    67â†’    const { measureGlassInteraction } = useGlassEffectPerformance('Button');
    68â†’

    70â†’    const setRefs = useCallback(
    71â†’      (node: HTMLButtonElement | null) => {
    72â†’        // Set internal ref
    73â†’        if (internalButtonRef.current !== node) {
    74â†’          (
    75â†’            internalButtonRef as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLButtonElement | null>

    82â†’        }

    85â†’          ref(node);

    96â†’

     Apple-style glass card
   </GlassCard>
   ```

   307â†’    deprecated: {
   308â†’      color: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800 dark:bg-red-900 dark:text-red-200',
   309â†’      icon: 'ğŸš«',
   310â†’      description: 'Will be removed in future versions',
   311â†’    },
   312â†’  };
   313â†’
   314â†’  const config = statusConfig[status];
   315â†’
   316â†’  return (
   317â†’    <div
   318â†’      className={cn(
   319â†’        'inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 rounded-full text-sm font-medium mb-4',
   320â†’        config.color
   321â†’      )}
   322â†’    >
   323â†’      <span>{config.icon}</span>
   324â†’      <span>Status: {status.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + status.slice(1)}</span>
   325â†’      <span className="text-xs opacity-75">â€” {config.description}</span>
   326â†’    </div>
   327â†’  );
   328â†’};
   329â†’

1â†’import React, { forwardRef, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
     2â†’import { motion, Variants } from 'framer-motion';
     3â†’import { cn } from '@/lib/glass-utils';
     4â†’import { useLiquidGlass, useContentAwareGlass } from '@/hooks/use-liquid-glass';
     5â†’import { useMagneticHover } from '@/lib/glass-physics';
     6â†’import { GlassButton } from './glass-button';
     7â†’import {
     8â†’  fadeInUpLarge,
     9â†’  containerFadeInFast,
    10â†’} from '@/lib/framer-motion-constants';
    11â†’
    12â†’export interface GlassHeroProps extends React.HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
    13â†’  title: string;
    14â†’  subtitle?: string;
    15â†’  description?: string;
    16â†’  primaryAction?: {
    17â†’    label: string;
    18â†’    onClick: () => void;
    19â†’    icon?: React.ReactNode;
    20â†’  };
    21â†’  secondaryAction?: {
    22â†’    label: string;
    23â†’    onClick: () => void;
    24â†’    icon?: React.ReactNode;
    25â†’  };
    26â†’  backgroundImage?: string;
    27â†’  backgroundVideo?: string;
    28â†’  variant?: 'default' | 'centered' | 'split' | 'minimal';
    29â†’  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl';
    30â†’  enableParallax?: boolean;
    31â†’  enableMagnetic?: boolean;
    32â†’}
    33â†’
    34â†’const GlassHero = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, GlassHeroProps>(
    35â†’  (
    36â†’    {
    37â†’      className,
    38â†’      title,
    39â†’      subtitle,
    40â†’      description,
    41â†’      primaryAction,
    42â†’      secondaryAction,
    43â†’      backgroundImage,
    44â†’      backgroundVideo,
    45â†’      variant = 'default',
    46â†’      size = 'lg',
    47â†’      enableParallax = true,
    48â†’      enableMagnetic = false,
    49â†’      children,
    50â†’      ...props
    51â†’    },
    52â†’    ref
    53â†’  ) => {
    54â†’    const contentRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
    55â†’    const { specularHighlights } = useLiquidGlass();
    56â†’    useContentAwareGlass(contentRef as React.RefObject<HTMLElement>);
    57â†’    const { elementRef: magneticRef, transform } = useMagneticHover(0.2, 200);
    58â†’
    59â†’    // Callback ref to handle both content and magnetic refs
    60â†’const setRefs = useCallback((node: HTMLDivElement | null) => {
    61â†’      (contentRef as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLDivElement | null>).current = node;
    62â†’      if (enableMagnetic && magneticRef) {
    63â†’        (magneticRef as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLElement | null>).current = node;
    64â†’      }
    65â†’      if (typeof ref === 'function') {
    66â†’        ref(node);
    67â†’      } else if (ref) {
    68â†’        (ref as React.MutableRefObject<HTMLDivElement | null>).current = node;
    69â†’      }
    70â†’    }, [enableMagnetic, magneticRef, ref]);
    71â†’
    72â†’    const sizeClasses = {
    73â†’      sm: 'min-h-[60vh] py-16 px-6',
    74â†’      md: 'min-h-[70vh] py-20 px-8',
    75â†’      lg: 'min-h-[80vh] py-24 px-8',
    76â†’      xl: 'min-h-[90vh] py-32 px-12',
    77â†’    };
    78â†’
    79â†’    const variantClasses = {
    80â†’      default: 'text-center',
    81â†’      centered: 'text-center items-center justify-center',
    82â†’      split: 'text-left lg:text-left items-center',
    83â†’      minimal: 'text-center items-center justify-center py-16',
    84â†’    };
    85â†’
    86â†’    const titleSizes = {
    87â†’      sm: 'text-4xl md:text-5xl',
    88â†’      md: 'text-5xl md:text-6xl',
    89â†’      lg: 'text-6xl md:text-7xl lg:text-8xl',
    90â†’      xl: 'text-7xl md:text-8xl lg:text-9xl',
    91â†’    };
    92â†’
    93â†’    const containerVariants: Variants = containerFadeInFast;
    94â†’
    95â†’    const itemVariants: Variants = fadeInUpLarge;
    96â†’
    97â†’    const parallaxVariants = enableParallax
    98â†’      ? {
    99â†’          initial: { y: 0 },
   100â†’          animate: { y: -20 },
   101â†’          transition: {
   102â†’            duration: 2,
   103â†’            repeat: Infinity,
   104â†’            repeatType: 'reverse' as const,
   105â†’            ease: 'easeInOut' as const,
   106â†’          },
   107â†’        }
   108â†’      : {};
   109â†’
   110â†’    return (
   111â†’      <div
   112â†’        ref={setRefs}
   113â†’        className={cn(
   114â†’          'relative overflow-hidden',
   115â†’          'liquid-glass-adaptive liquid-glass-depth-2',
   116â†’          specularHighlights && 'liquid-glass-specular',
   117â†’          sizeClasses[size],
   118â†’          className
   119â†’        )}
   120â†’        style={{
   121â†’          transform: enableMagnetic ? transform : undefined,
   122â†’          backgroundImage: backgroundImage
   123â†’            ? `url(${backgroundImage})`
   124â†’            : 'linear-gradient(135deg, #1a1a1a 0%, #2d2d2d 20%, #4a4a4a 40%, #6b7280 60%, #9ca3af 80%, #e5e7eb 100%)',
   125â†’          backgroundSize: backgroundImage ? 'cover' : '400% 400%',
   126â†’          backgroundPosition: 'center',
   127â†’          backgroundAttachment: enableParallax ? 'fixed' : 'scroll',
   128â†’          animation: !backgroundImage
   129â†’            ? 'gradientShift 15s ease infinite'
   130â†’            : undefined,
   131â†’        }}
   132â†’        {...props}
   133â†’      >
   134â†’        {/* Background Video */}
   135â†’        {backgroundVideo && (
   136â†’          <video
   137â†’            autoPlay
