    63â†’    filter: 'blur(1px) drop-shadow(10px 4px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3)) brightness(115%)',
    64â†’  },
    65â†’  strong: {
    66â†’    boxShadow: 'inset -14px -12px 0px -15px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1), inset 0px -13px 0px -12px rgba(255, 255, 255, 1)',
    67â†’    filter: 'blur(1.5px) drop-shadow(14px 6px 8px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4)) brightness(120%)',
    68â†’  },
    69â†’} as const;
    70â†’
    71â†’/**
    72â†’ * Enhanced Hook for Apple liquid glass magnetic hover effect
    73â†’ * Updated with React 19 patterns and performance optimizations
    74â†’ */
    75â†’export function useAppleLiquidGlass(options: AppleLiquidGlassOptions = {}) {
    76â†’  const elementRef = useRef<HTMLElement>(null);
    77â†’  const {
    78â†’    intensity = 'medium',
    79â†’    magneticStrength = 0.3,
    80â†’    liquidFlow = true,
    81â†’    enableHaptics = false,
    82â†’    multiLayer = false,
    83â†’    animated = false,
    84â†’    distortionEffect = false,
    85â†’  } = options;
    86â†’
    87â†’  const handleMouseMove = useCallback((e: MouseEvent) => {
    88â†’    if (!elementRef.current) return;
    89â†’
    90â†’    // Use startTransition for smooth animations
    91â†’    startTransition(() => {
    92â†’      const rect = elementRef.current!.getBoundingClientRect();
    93â†’      const centerX = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
    94â†’      const centerY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
    95â†’      
    96â†’      const deltaX = (e.clientX - centerX) * magneticStrength;
    97â†’      const deltaY = (e.clientY - centerY) * magneticStrength;
    98â†’
    99â†’      elementRef.current!.style.transform = `translate(${deltaX}px, ${deltaY}px) translateZ(0)`;
   100â†’      
   101â†’      if (liquidFlow && multiLayer) {
   102â†’        // Enhanced liquid flow for multi-layer structure
   103â†’        const glassFilter = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-filter') as HTMLElement;
   104â†’        const glassOverlay = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-overlay') as HTMLElement;
   105â†’        
   106â†’        if (glassFilter) {
   107â†’          glassFilter.style.transform = `translate(${-deltaX * 0.2}px, ${-deltaY * 0.2}px)`;
   108â†’        }
   109â†’        
   110â†’        if (glassOverlay) {
   111â†’          glassOverlay.style.transform = `translate(${-deltaX * 0.1}px, ${-deltaY * 0.1}px)`;
   112â†’        }
   113â†’      }
   114â†’    });
   115â†’  }, [magneticStrength, liquidFlow, multiLayer]);
   116â†’
   117â†’  const handleMouseLeave = useCallback(() => {
   118â†’    if (!elementRef.current) return;
   119â†’    
   120â†’    startTransition(() => {
   121â†’      elementRef.current!.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px) translateZ(0)';
   122â†’      elementRef.current!.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   123â†’      
   124â†’      if (multiLayer) {
   125â†’        const glassFilter = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-filter') as HTMLElement;
   126â†’        const glassOverlay = elementRef.current!.querySelector('.glass-overlay') as HTMLElement;
   127â†’        
   128â†’        if (glassFilter) {
   129â†’          glassFilter.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px)';
   130â†’          glassFilter.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   131â†’        }
   132â†’        
   133â†’        if (glassOverlay) {
   134â†’          glassOverlay.style.transform = 'translate(0px, 0px)';
   135â†’          glassOverlay.style.transition = 'transform 0.5s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)';
   136â†’        }
   137â†’      }
   138â†’      
   139â†’      setTimeout(() => {
   140â†’        if (elementRef.current) {
   141â†’          elementRef.current.style.transition = '';
   142â†’          
   143â†’          if (multiLayer) {
   144â†’            const glassFilter = elementRef.current.querySelector('.glass-filter') as HTMLElement;
   145â†’            const glassOverlay = elementRef.current.querySelector('.glass-overlay') as HTMLElement;
   146â†’            
   147â†’            if (glassFilter) glassFilter.style.transition = '';
   148â†’            if (glassOverlay) glassOverlay.style.transition = '';
   149â†’          }
   150â†’        }
   151â†’      }, 500);
   152â†’    });
   153â†’
   154â†’    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   155â†’      navigator.vibrate(10);
   156â†’    }
   157â†’  }, [enableHaptics, multiLayer]);
   158â†’
   159â†’  const handleMouseEnter = useCallback(() => {
   160â†’    if (enableHaptics && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
   161â†’      navigator.vibrate(5);
   162â†’    }
   163â†’  }, [enableHaptics]);
   164â†’
   165â†’  useEffect(() => {
   166â†’    const element = elementRef.current;
   167â†’    if (!element) return;
   168â†’
   169â†’    element.addEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   170â†’    element.addEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   171â†’    element.addEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   172â†’
   173â†’    return () => {
   174â†’      element.removeEventListener('mousemove', handleMouseMove);
   175â†’      element.removeEventListener('mouseleave', handleMouseLeave);
   176â†’      element.removeEventListener('mouseenter', handleMouseEnter);
   177â†’    };
   178â†’  }, [handleMouseMove, handleMouseLeave, handleMouseEnter]);
   179â†’
   180â†’  return {
   181â†’    ref: elementRef,
   182â†’    variant: APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS[intensity],
   183â†’    shadow: APPLE_LIQUID_SHADOWS[intensity],
   184â†’    afterEffect: APPLE_LIQUID_AFTER_EFFECTS[intensity],
   185â†’    multiLayer,
   186â†’    animated,
   187â†’    distortionEffect,
   188â†’  };
   189â†’}
   190â†’
   191â†’/**
   192â†’ * Generate Apple liquid glass CSS classes - Tailwind v4 Compatible
   193â†’ * Enhanced with multi-layer and new effect options
   194â†’ */
   195â†’export function getAppleLiquidGlassClass(
   196â†’  intensity: keyof typeof APPLE_LIQUID_VARIANTS = 'medium',
   197â†’  options: {
   198â†’    interactive?: boolean;
   199â†’    magnetic?: boolean;
   200â†’    animated?: boolean;
   201â†’    multiLayer?: boolean;
   202â†’  } = {}
   203â†’): string {
   204â†’  const { interactive = true, magnetic = false, animated = false, multiLayer = false } = options;
   205â†’  
   206â†’  const baseClass = 'apple-liquid-glass';
   207â†’  const intensityClass = intensity !== 'medium' ? `apple-liquid-glass--${intensity}` : '';
   208â†’  const interactiveClass = interactive ? 'apple-liquid-glass--interactive' : '';
   209â†’  const magneticClass = magnetic ? 'apple-liquid-glass--magnetic' : '';
   210â†’  const animatedClass = animated ? 'apple-liquid-glass--animated' : '';
   211â†’  
   212â†’  return [baseClass, intensityClass, interactiveClass, magneticClass, animatedClass].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
   213â†’}
   214â†’
   215â†’/**
   216â†’ * Generate multi-layer glass structure JSX
   217â†’ * For use with the new multi-layer glass components
   218â†’ */
   219â†’export function createGlassLayers(content: React.ReactNode, className?: string): React.ReactNode {
   220â†’  return React.createElement(
   221â†’    React.Fragment,
   222â†’    null,
   223â†’    React.createElement('div', { className: 'glass-filter' }),
   224â†’    React.createElement('div', { className: 'glass-overlay' }),
   225â†’    React.createElement('div', { className: 'glass-specular' }),
   226â†’    React.createElement('div', { className: `glass-content ${className || ''}` }, content)
   227â†’  );
   228â†’}
   229â†’
   230â†’/**
   231â†’ * Apple liquid glass animation presets
   232â†’ */
   233â†’export const APPLE_LIQUID_ANIMATIONS = {
   234â†’  hover: {
   235â†’    transform: 'translateY(-2px)',
   236â†’    transition: 'all 0.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   237â†’  },
   238â†’  active: {
   239â†’    transform: 'translateY(0px) scale(0.98)',
   240â†’    transition: 'all 0.15s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   241â†’  },
   242â†’  focus: {
   243â†’    boxShadow: '0 0 0 3px rgba(0, 122, 255, 0.3)',
   244â†’    transition: 'box-shadow 0.2s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   245â†’  },
   246â†’} as const;
